 Navaratri specifically prescribes the worship of various forms of mother
 ajanvaratrika aakhri din he or aaj ke din bhikanya pujanaka vishesh mahatv hota he
 On this day girls from two years to 10 years are worshiped
 alag-algaumraki kanyaayein devi ke alag-alag rup ko darshaati hai
 Only after worshiping the nine girls as a reflection of the nine goddesses, the devotees' Kanavratravratha is completed
 jaane,navamike din kanya pujan kashubh muhurtakya he?pehla muhoort-subah 6 bajkar 29 minute se 7 bajkar 54 minute tak
 Second Muhurta - 10 AM to 46 AM, 3 PM to 3 PM
 kanya pujan kii vidhi-- kanya bhoj or pujan ke liye kanyaon ko ek din pehle hi aamantrit kar diya jaataa he
 - It is not right to catch girls from here and there on the main Kanyapujan day
 - grih pravesh par kanyaon kaa puure parivaar ke saath pushp varsha se swaagat karen or nav durga ke sabhi nau naamon ke jayakaare lagaaein
 Now, these girls should sit in a comfortable and clean place and place their feet in a plate or plate filled with milk and wash their feet with their hands and should be blessed by touching their feet
 - uske baad maathe par akshat, phool or kumkum lagaana chahie

 - bhojan ke baad kanyaon ko apane samarthy ke anusaar dakshina, uphaar den or unke punah pair chhukar ashish len
 Worshiping the female form according to age - Navaratri is worshiped on all the dates one by one and on Ashtami or Navami nine girls are worshiped
 - do varsh kii kanya (kumari) ke pujan se dukh or daridrata maa dur karti hai

 isaki puja se parivaar kaa kalyaan hota he

 - The girl of six years is called Kalika Roop

 - The eight-year-old girl is called Shambhavi
 iskaa pujan karne se vaad-vivaad main vijay praapt hoti he
 The nine-year-old girl is called Durga

 - The ten year old girl is called Subhadra

 mal ke kisi bhi floor par aisi koi vyavastha nahin thi
 When i asked the mall employee, he said to be feeding in the toilet

 Arvind was a medical lab technician himself, so Sonia had no reason to be surprised or denied it
 sonia injection lene ke liye taiyaar ho gai or udhar arvind ne isi injection ke raste apni bivi kii ragon main maut ghol diya

 ab usne iske liye duusari sajeesh rachi

 ek lab technitian hone ke naate wo khun nikaalnaa or injection lagaana bakhubi jaanata tha

 ek or gahari chalsui ke kaaran sonia ab dhire-dhire wo biimaar rahane lagi

 phir ek roj usne duusari sajeesh rachi
